"Tettili" means "it is". **Important Considerations:** * **Regional Variation:** Central Atlas Tamazight has considerable regional variation. This translation aims for a relatively standard form, but a speaker from a specific valley might phrase it slightly differently. * **Technical Terminology:** Translating scientific terms like "carotenoid" directly into Tamazight can be difficult.
